main.cpp!
 
#include <ilcplex/ilocplex.h> 
#include "readfile.h" 
#include "parameters.h" 
#include "runGraph.h" 
#include "time_calc.h" 
#include "crew.h" 
 
#include <iostream> 
#include <fstream> 
#include <string> 
#include <sstream> 
#include <vector> 
#include <iomanip> 
#include <time.h> 
 
 
ILOSTLBEGIN 
 
using namespace std; 
 
typedef IloArray<IloNumVarArray>  IloNumVarArray2; 
 
 
 
int 
main(int, char**) 
{ 
     
    start = clock(); 
    start_Graph = clock(); 
         
    runGraph();                                                             // Construct the graph 
         
    end_Graph = clock(); 
     
     
    
    start_Crew = clock(); 
     
     
    crew_start();                   // Create the initial calculation for the original crew schedule 
    crew_end(allCorr);              // Make the mapping to Corr in order to control 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < allCorr.size(); i++) 
    { 
        cout << allCorr[i].getCap() << " " << allCorr[i].getDuty() << " " << allCorr[i].getID() << " " << 
allCorr[i].getArc() << endl; 
    } 
     
    cout << endl; 
     
    crew_matrix(allCorr, allNodes, allArcs);   // Create the relation between violation connections between arcs 
     
    end_Crew = clock(); 
     
     
     
         
         
 // 
     
    start_Cplex = clock(); 
     
     
    IloEnv env;                                                             // Enter CPLEX environment 
     
     
    try { 
         
        IloModel model(env);                                                // Initialise model object 
         
        IloNumVarArray var_y(env, nbFlights,0,1,ILOBOOL);                   // Initalise y[n] 
         
        vector<int> arcin;                                                  // Create vector storing arcs in the 
objective fct 
         
        int no_constr; 
         
        IloNumVarArray2 var_x(env);                                         // Initialise x[i][a] 
        for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) { 
            var_x.add(IloNumVarArray(env, allArcs.size(),0,1,ILOBOOL)); 
        } 
         
        IloExpr assign_cost(env), cancel_cost(env), uap_cost(env), add_cost(env);                         // Generate 
==PAGE:147==
cost parameters 
         
        for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
        { 
            for (int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++ ) 
            { 
                for (int j = 0; j < cost_arc[i].size(); j++) 
                { 
                    if (a == cost_arc[i][j]) 
                    { 
                        assign_cost += cost_factor[i][a] * var_x[i][a]; 
                        arcin.push_back(a); 
                     
                    } 
                } 
            } 
        } 
         
        for (int n = 0; n < nbFlights; n++)                                 // Create cancellation fee (2000) 
        { 
            cancel_cost += 2000*var_y[n]; 
        } 
         
        for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
        { 
            for (int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++) 
            { 
                if ((allArcs[a].getAir() == aircrafts[i]) && (allArcs[a].getType2() == "Original")) // The true flight 
                { 
                    uap_cost+= cChange*(1-var_x[i][a]);   // 16 flights (including maintenance) 
                } 
            } 
        } 
         
        unsigned int total; 
        total = arc1_connect.size()+arc1_duty.size()+arc1_rest.size(); 
         
        IloNumVarArray var_t(env, total, 0, 1, ILOBOOL); 
         
         
        for (int i = 0; i < total; i++) 
        { 
            add_cost+= cReserve*var_t[i]; 
        } 
         
        // Create objective function by adding it to the model 
         
        model.add(IloMinimize(env, assign_cost + cancel_cost + uap_cost + add_cost)); 
        assign_cost.end(); 
        cancel_cost.end(); 
         
         
        // Name decision variables: 
         
         
        var_y.setNames("y"); 
         
        char buffer[15]; 
         
         
        for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
        { 
            for (unsigned int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++ ) 
            { 
                sprintf(buffer, "x(%s,%d)", aircrafts[i].c_str(), a); 
                var_x[i][a].setName(buffer); 
                 
                     
            } 
        } 
         
        // Constraint 1 (flow) 
         
        for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++)               // for all i (aircraft) 
        { 
            for (unsigned int v = 0; v < allNodes.size(); v++)      // for all v (nodes) 
            { 
                if ((allNodes[v].getTime() <= rec_end+turntime) && (allNodes[v].getTime() >= rec_start)) // restriction 
                { 
                     
                 
                IloExpr constr1_lhs(env); 
                IloExpr constr1_rhs(env); 
                 
                for (unsigned int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++) {  // Sum up all a's that comply with the LHS 
                     
                     
                    // LHS 
                     
                    for (int j = 0; j < v_out[v].size(); j++) 
                    { 
                        if (a == v_out[v][j]) 
==PAGE:148==
                        { 
                            constr1_lhs+= var_x[i][a];              // All outgoing arcs from node v 
                             
                             
                        } 
                    } 
                     
                    // RHS 
                     
                    for (int j = 0; j < v_in[v].size(); j++) 
                    { 
                        if (a == v_in[v][j]) 
                        { 
                            constr1_rhs+= var_x[i][a];              // All ingoing arcs to node v 
                        } 
                    } 
                     
                } 
                 
                for (int j = 0; j < dem_arc[i].size(); j++) 
                 
                { 
                  
                    if (v == dem_arc[i][j]) 
                     
                    { 
                        constr1_rhs+= dem_factor[i][j];             // If node v has a demand for aircraft i 
                     
                    } 
                     
                } 
                 
                char buffer[30]; 
                sprintf(buffer, "Flow balance for node: %d", v);    // Name and add constraint 
                 
                IloConstraint c1(constr1_lhs == constr1_rhs); 
                c1.setName(buffer); 
                model.add(c1); 
                constr1_rhs.end(); 
                constr1_lhs.end(); 
                    no_constr++; 
                 
                } 
            } 
        } 
         
        // Constraint 2 (fly flight or cancel) 
         
       for (unsigned int n = 0; n < nbFlights; n++)                 // For all n (flights) 
        { 
             
             
            IloExpr constr2(env); 
                 
                for (unsigned int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++)   // Sum over a 
                { 
                    for (int j = 0; j < fl_arc[n].size();j++){ 
                         
                        if (a == fl_arc[n][j]) 
                        { 
                            for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++)    // Sum over i 
                            { 
                                constr2+= var_x[i][a]; 
                            } 
                         
                        } 
                    } 
                 
                } 
            constr2+= var_y[n];                                     // Name and add constraint 
            IloConstraint c2(constr2 == 1); 
            c2.setName("Allocation"); 
            model.add(c2); 
            constr2.end(); 
            no_constr++; 
             
        } 
         
         
        // Constraint 3 (assign fixed values) 
         
        for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++)               // Sum over i 
        { 
             
            for (unsigned int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++)       // Sum over a 
            { 
                 
                for (int j = 0; j < fix[i].size(); j++)             // Sum only for special arcs 
                { 
                     
                    if (a == fix[i][j])                             // Set to 1s 
                    { 
==PAGE:149==
                         
                        IloExpr constr3(env); 
                        constr3+= var_x[i][a]; 
                        IloConstraint c3(constr3 == 1); 
                        c3.setName("Fixed"); 
                        model.add(c3); 
                        constr3.end(); 
                        no_constr++; 
 
                    } 
                } 
                 
               if ((allArcs[a].getType2() == "First") && (allNodes[allArcs[a].getDepNode()].getType2() == "Source")) // 
Set others to 0 
                { 
                     
                        if (allNodes[allArcs[a].getDepNode()].getAir() != aircrafts[i]) 
                        { 
                            IloExpr constr4(env); 
                            constr4+= var_x[i][a]; 
                            IloConstraint c4(constr4 == 0); 
                            c4.setName("Source"); 
                            model.add(c4); 
                            constr4.end(); 
                            no_constr++; 
                        } 
 
                     
                } 
                 
            } 
             
             
        } 
            
 
         
        
         
        // Constraint 4 (Crew - Duty time) 
         
        for (int a = 0; a < arc1_duty.size(); a++){   // A constraint for each arc-arc pair needs to be created 
             
            IloExpr constr5(env); 
             
            for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) // Sum over aircraft (all included) as seen as independent 
            { 
                constr5+= var_x[i][arc1_duty[a]]; 
            } 
             
             
            IloConstraint c5(constr5 <= var_t[a]);                     // Name and add constraint 
            c5.setName("Duty"); 
            model.add(c5); 
            constr5.end(); 
            no_constr++; 
        } 
         
        // Constraint 5 (Crew - Rest time) 
         
        for (int a = 0; a < arc1_rest.size(); a++){   // A constraint for each arc-arc pair needs to be created 
             
            IloExpr constr6(env); 
             
            for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) // Sum over aircraft (all included) as seen as independent 
            { 
                constr6+= var_x[i][arc1_rest[a]]+var_x[i][arc2_rest[a]]; 
            } 
             
             
            IloConstraint c6(constr6 <= 1 + var_t[arc1_duty.size() + a]);                     // Name and add 
constraint 
            c6.setName("Rest"); 
            model.add(c6); 
            constr6.end(); 
            no_constr++; 
        } 
         
        // Constraint 6 (Crew - Connection time) 
         
        for (int a = 0; a < arc1_connect.size(); a++){   // A constraint for each arc-arc pair needs to be created 
             
            IloExpr constr7(env); 
             
            for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) // Sum over aircraft (all included) as seen as independent 
            { 
                constr7+= var_x[i][arc1_connect[a]]+var_x[i][arc2_connect[a]]; 
            } 
             
             
            IloConstraint c7(constr7 <= 1 + var_t[arc1_duty.size() + arc1_rest.size() + a]); 
            c7.setName("Connect"); 
==PAGE:150==
            model.add(c7); 
            constr7.end(); 
            no_constr++; 
        } 
         
        // Fix non HUB departures 
  
         
        for (int i = 0; i < arc1_duty.size(); i++) 
        { 
            if (allArcs[arc1_duty[i]].getDepName() != "HUB")  // If none of them departs from stockholm 
            { 
                IloExpr constr8(env); 
                constr8+= var_t[i]; 
                IloConstraint c8(constr8 == 0); 
                c8.setName("Not HUB"); 
                model.add(c8); 
                constr8.end(); 
                no_constr++; 
            } 
        } 
         
        for (int i = 0; i < arc1_rest.size(); i++) 
        { 
            if ((allArcs[arc1_rest[i]].getDepName() != "HUB") && 
                (allArcs[arc2_rest[i]].getDepName() != "HUB"))   // If none of them departs from stockholm 
            { 
                IloExpr constr8(env); 
                constr8+= var_t[i+arc1_duty.size()]; 
                IloConstraint c8(constr8 == 0); 
                c8.setName("Not HUB"); 
                model.add(c8); 
                constr8.end(); 
                no_constr++; 
            } 
        } 
         
         
        for (int i = 0; i < arc1_connect.size(); i++) 
        { 
            if ((allArcs[arc1_connect[i]].getDepName() != "HUB") && 
                (allArcs[arc2_connect[i]].getDepName() != "HUB"))   // If none of them departs from stockholm 
            { 
                IloExpr constr8(env); 
                constr8+= var_t[i + arc1_duty.size() + arc1_rest.size()]; 
                IloConstraint c8(constr8 == 0); 
                c8.setName("Not HUB"); 
                model.add(c8); 
                constr8.end(); 
                no_constr++; 
            } 
        } 
       
    
   
         
         
         
        sort(arcin.begin(), arcin.end());  // Sort vector 
        arcin.erase(unique(arcin.begin(), arcin.end()),arcin.end()); // Erase non-unique values 
         
        // Disruption case 
        // Only for arcs within recovery window is a disruption case allowed 
         
        // if (((allArcs[a].getArrName() == "AP6") || (allArcs[a].getDepName() == "AP6")) 
       // && ((allNodes[allArcs[a].getDepNode()].getTime() >= 500) && (allNodes[allArcs[a].getDepNode()].getTime() <= 
800))) 
 
        
         
         
        for (int n = 0; n < nbFlights; n++) 
        { 
            for (int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++) 
            { 
                for (int j = 0; j < fl_arc[n].size(); j++) 
                { 
                    if (a == fl_arc[n][j]) 
                    { 
                        for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
                        { 
                            if ((allArcs[a].getDepName() == "HUB") && 
                                (allNodes[allArcs[a].getDepNode()].getTime() >= 810) && 
                                (allNodes[allArcs[a].getDepNode()].getTime() <= 960) && 
                                (allArcs[a].getType2() != "Maintenance")) 
                            { 
                                disruption(i,a,var_x,model); // Create disruption through disruption function 
                                // no_constr++; 
                            } 
                        } 
                    }

                } 
                 
            } 
        } 
         
        for (int n = 0; n < nbFlights; n++) 
        { 
            for (int a = 0; a < allArcs.size(); a++) 
            { 
                for (int j = 0; j < fl_arc[n].size(); j++) 
                { 
                    if (a == fl_arc[n][j]) 
                    { 
                        for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
                        { 
                            if ((allArcs[a].getArrName() == "HUB") &&

        IloCplex cplex(env);                             // Create and solve CPLEX model 
   
        cplex.extract(model); 
        cplex.exportModel("Model.lp"); 
        cplex.solve(); 
         
        end_Cplex = clock();                                        // End time 
         
  
         
        start_Illo = clock(); 
 
        // Print solution 
         
        cout << endl << "CPLEX SOLUTION" << endl; 
         
        for (int i = 0; i < 35; i++){ cout << "--"; } 
        cout << endl << endl; 
         
        cout << left << setw(16) << "Objective value" << right << setw(10) << cplex.getObjValue() << endl; 
        cout << left << setw(16) << "Status" << right << setw(10) << cplex.getStatus() << endl; 
        cout << endl; 
         
         
         
        // Print solution 
         
cout << endl << "Changes in schedule:" << endl << "-------------------------" << endl; 
         
        k = 0; 
         
         
        for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
        { 
            for (unsigned int j = 0; j < Org[i].size(); j++) 
            { 
                if (cplex.getValue(var_x[i][Org[i][j]] != 1)) 
                    { 
                        cout << aircrafts[i] << "\t" << Org[i][j] << endl; 
                        k++; 
                    } 
            } 
        } 
         
        if (k == 0) 
        { 
            cout << "No changes in schedule" << endl; 
        } 
         
        for (int i = 0; i < 35; i++){ cout << "--"; } 
        cout << endl; 
         
        cout << endl << "Cancellation of flights:" << endl << "-------------------------" << endl; 
         
        k = 0; 
         
==PAGE:152==
        for (int n = 0; n < nbFlights; n++) 
        { 
                if (cplex.getValue(var_y[n]) > 0) 
                { 
                    cout << flightRoute[n] << endl; 
                    k++; 
 
                } 
        } 
             
        if (k == 0) 
        { 
            cout << "No cancellations" << endl; 
        } 
         
        for (int i = 0; i < 35; i++){ cout << "--"; } 
        cout << endl; 
         
        int count; 
         
        end = clock(); 
         
        time(end,start,end_Graph,start_Graph,end_Cplex,start_Cplex, start_Crew, end_Crew, start_Illo, end_Illo);                
// Calculate and print time variables 
         
        for (int i = 0; i < total; i++) 
        { 
            if (cplex.getValue(var_t[i]) > 0) 
            { 
                count++; 
                 
                if (i < arc1_duty.size()){ 
                    cout << "Violation " << count << " is " << i << "duty " << allArcs[arc1_duty[i]].getCap() << endl; 
                } 
                if ((i < arc1_duty.size()+arc1_rest.size()) && (i >= arc1_duty.size())){ 
                    cout << "Violation " << count << " is " << i << "rest " << allArcs[arc1_rest[i]].getCap() << endl; 
                } 
                if ((i < total) && (i >= arc1_duty.size()+arc1_rest.size())){ 
                    cout << "Violation " << count << " is " << i << "connect " << allArcs[arc1_connect[i]].getCap() << 
endl; 
                } 
            } 
        } 
        cout << "Number of violations " << count << endl; 
         
        end_Illo = clock(); 
         
        cout << endl << "Number of decision variables: " << nbFlights + nbFlights*nbAircraft + arcin.size()*nbAircraft 
+ total << endl; 
        cout << "Number of constraints " << no_constr << endl; 
         
    } 
    catch (IloException& ex) { 
        cerr << "Error: " << ex << endl; 
    } 
    catch (...) { 
        cerr << "Error" << endl; 
    } 
    env.end();   
     
    return 0; 
}

#ifndef runGraph_h 
#define runGraph_h 
 
#include <iostream> 
#include <fstream> 
#include <string> 
#include <sstream> 
#include <vector> 
#include <iomanip>

using namespace std; 
 
// Global variables 
 
vector<Nodes> allNodes;                                             // Construct Nodes (initiate) 
 
vector<Arcs> allArcs;                                               // Construct Arcs (initiate) 
 
vector<Corr> allCorr;                                               // Construct correlation between crew, duties, ids 
and arcs 
 
 
void runGraph(void){ 
     
   
   readFile1("data_3.txt");                  // Read in data (Windows Formatted Text) 
     
    allocateData(dataArray1);              // Allocate data values from file to arrays 
     
     
 
     
    createNodes(allNodes, "Departure", "Original");              // Create departure and arrival nodes for org. flights 
     
    createNodes(allNodes, "Arrival", "Original"); 
     
    createNodes(allNodes, "Departure", "Delay");                // Create departure and arrival nodes for delay flights 
     
    createNodes(allNodes, "Arrival", "Delay");

    createNodes(allNodes,"Arrival", "Maintenance"); 
     
     
 
     
    createArcs_Flight(allNodes, allArcs, "Original");               // Create flight arcs for original flights, delays

    create_delay_arcs(allNodes, allArcs); 
     
    createArcs_Flight(allNodes,allArcs, "Maintenance"); 
     
     
     
    source_index(allNodes);                                         // Identify where to place source and sink nodes 
     
    sink_index(allNodes); 
     
    rec_source_index(allNodes);                                     // Recovery window source/sink nodes 
     
    rec_sink_index(allNodes); 
     
    rec_source_index2(allNodes);  
     
     
    rec_source_nodes(allNodes); 
     
    rec_after_index(allNodes); 
     
    rec_sink_nodes(allNodes); 
     
    sink_arc_node(allNodes);

    sink_arc(allNodes, allArcs); 
     
    first_departure(allNodes); 
     
    createArcs_first(allNodes,allArcs);                             // Create arcs from arrival to first possible 
departure 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAirports; i++){ 
        air_dep(allNodes, allArcs, airports[i]);                    // Create arc from departure node to the sequential 
dep node 
    }                                                               // at the same airport 
     
 
     
     
    org_alloc(allArcs);                                             // Create original assignment 
     
    org_alloc_cap(allArcs);                                         // Crew original assignment (to arcs) 
     
    adj_alloc(allNodes,allArcs);                                    // Adjacency "matrix 
     
    cost_alloc(allArcs);                                            // Create cost "matrix" 
     
    flight_alloc(allArcs);                                          // Create flight to arc index 
     
    demand_alloc(allNodes);                                         // Create demand "matrix" 
     
    in_go(allNodes, allArcs); 
     
    out_go(allNodes, allArcs);

// and thereby create an illustration of the graph network 
 
    ganttplot(allNodes, allArcs);

vector<int> arc2_connect; 
 
 
 
 
// Allocation of data  ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
 
 
void allocateData(string dataArray[size][size]){ 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        strt[i] = atoi(dataArray[i][dataSt].c_str()); 
    } 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        et[i] = atoi(dataArray[i][dataEt].c_str()); 
==PAGE:157==
    } 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        departure[i] = dataArray[i][dataDep]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        destination[i] = dataArray[i][dataDes]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        aircraftassigned[i] = dataArray[i][dataAir]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        flightRoute[i] = dataArray[i][dataID]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        fleetReq[i] = dataArray[i][dataFleet]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAirports; i++){ 
        airports[i] = dataArray[i][dataAirport]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++){ 
        aircrafts[i] = dataArray[i][dataAircraft]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++){ 
        fleettype[i] = dataArray[i][dataFleetType]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        cap[i] = dataArray[i][dataCaptain]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbCaptains; i++){ 
        captains[i] = dataArray[i][dataCaptains]; 
    } 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
        dut[i] = dataArray[i][dataDut]; 
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbDuties; i++){ 
        duties[i] = dataArray[i][dataDuties]; 
    } 
     
     
     
     
     
    // Captains to IDs 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++) 
    { 
        for (int c = 0; c < nbCaptains; c++) 
        { 
            if(cap[i] == captains[c]) 
            { 
                cap_fl[c].push_back(flightRoute[i]); 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
    // Captains to Duty times 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++) 
    { 
        for (int c = 0; c < nbCaptains; c++) 
        { 
            if(cap[i] == captains[c]) 
            { 
                cap_duty[c].push_back(dut[i]); 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
    // Duties to IDs 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbActivities; i++) 
    { 
        for (int c = 0; c < nbDuties; c++) 
        { 
            if(dut[i] == duties[c]) 
            { 
                id_duty[c].push_back(flightRoute[i]); 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
     
 
}

createGraph.h!
#ifndef createGraph_h 
#define createGraph_h 
 
#include <iostream> 
#include <fstream> 
#include <string>

// Create all nodes (excl. source and sink nodes) ----------------------------------------------------------------- 
 
void createNodes(vector<Nodes>& newClass, string type1, string type2){ 
     
    string airport; 
    float time; 
    string id; 
    string air; 
    string fleet; 
    float start; 
    string captain; 
    string duty; 
     
    if(type2 == "Original"){                                            // Create original nodes 
         
        for(int i = 0; i < nbFlights; i++){ 
            if (type1 == "Departure") {                                 // Original departure nodes 
                airport = departure[i]; 
                time = strt[i]; 
                id = flightRoute[i]; 
                air = aircraftassigned[i]; 
                fleet = fleetReq[i]; 
                captain = cap[i]; 
                duty = dut[i]; 
            } else {                                                    // Original arrival ndoes 
                airport = destination[i]; 
                time = et[i]; 
                id = flightRoute[i]; 
                air = aircraftassigned[i]; 
                fleet = fleetReq[i]; 
                captain = cap[i]; 
                duty = dut[i]; 
            } 
             
             
            Nodes newNode(type1, type2, airport, time, id, air, fleet, captain, duty); 
            newClass.push_back(newNode);                                // Add the newNode to the node-vector 
             
        } 
    } else if(type2 == "Delay"){                                        // Create delay nodes (depending on the no. of 
delays) 
         
        int j = 0; 
        while (j <= nbDelays){ 
             
            for(int i = 0; i < nbFlights; i++){ 
                if (type1 == "Departure") { 
                    airport = departure[i]; 
                    time = strt[i] + delayInterval*pow(2.0,j); 
                    id = flightRoute[i]; 
                    air = aircraftassigned[i]; 
                    fleet = fleetReq[i]; 
                    start = strt[i]; 
                    captain = cap[i]; 
                    duty = dut[i]; 
                } else { 
                    airport = destination[i]; 
                    time = et[i] + delayInterval*pow(2.0,j); 
                    id = flightRoute[i]; 
                    air = aircraftassigned[i]; 
                    fleet = fleetReq[i]; 
                    start = strt[i]; 
                    captain = cap[i]; 
                    duty = dut[i]; 
                } 
                 
==PAGE:159==
                if((time >= rec_start) && (time <= rec_end) && (start >= rec_start))  // Time window 
                { 
                    Nodes newNode(type1, type2, airport, time, id, air, fleet, captain, duty, j+1); 
                    newClass.push_back(newNode);   // Add the newNode to the node-vector 
                } 
            } 
            j++; 
        } 
         
         
    } else if(type2 == "Maintenance"){ 
         
        for(int i = nbFlights; i < nbActivities; i++){ 
             
            if (type1 == "Departure") {                                 // Original departure nodes 
                airport = departure[i]; 
                time = strt[i]; 
                id = flightRoute[i]; 
                air = aircraftassigned[i]; 
                fleet = fleetReq[i]; 
                captain = cap[i]; 
                duty = dut[i]; 
            } else {                                                    // Original arrival ndoes 
                airport = destination[i]; 
                time = et[i]; 
                id = flightRoute[i]; 
                air = aircraftassigned[i]; 
                fleet = fleetReq[i]; 
                captain = cap[i]; 
                duty = dut[i]; 
            } 
             
            
             
            Nodes newNode(type1, type2, airport, time, id, air, fleet, captain, duty); 
            newClass.push_back(newNode); 
           
             
        } 
    } 
     
} 
 
 
 
// Identify the first activity for all aircrafts --------------------------------------------------------- 
 
void source_index(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass) { 
     
    int time; // set to big value 
     
    for (int j = 0; j < nbAircraft; j++) { 
         
        time = 20000; 
         
        for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++){ 
             
            if(nodeClass[i].getAir() == aircrafts[j]){    // If aircraft is matched 
                 
                if(nodeClass[i].getTime() < time){        // If time is less than previous time 
                     
                    sourceIndex[j] = i; 
                     
                    time = nodeClass[i].getTime(); 
                } 
            } 
             
        } 
         
    } 
     
} 
 
// Identify the last activitiy for all aircraft --------------------------------------------------------- 
 
void sink_index(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass) { 
     
    int time; // set to big value 
     
    for (int j = 0; j < nbAircraft; j++) { 
         
        time = 0; 
         
        for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++){ 
             
            if(nodeClass[i].getAir() == aircrafts[j]){    // If aircraft is matched 
                 
                if(nodeClass[i].getTime() > time){        // If time is bigger than previous time 
                     
                    sinkIndex[j] = i; 
                     
                    time = nodeClass[i].getTime(); 
==PAGE:160==
                } 
            } 
             
        } 
         
    } 
     
} 
 
 
// Create delay arcs 
 
void create_delay_arcs(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass){ 
     
     
     
    for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++) // Departure nodes 
    { 
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < nodeClass.size(); j++) // Arrival nodes 
        { 
             
            if ( (nodeClass[i].getType1() == "Departure") && (nodeClass[j].getType1() == "Arrival") && 
(nodeClass[i].getType2() == "Delay") && (nodeClass[j].getType2() == "Delay")) // A departure to an arrival that both 
are delay nodes 
            { 
                 
                if ((nodeClass[i].getAir() == nodeClass[j].getAir()) && (nodeClass[i].getDelay() == 
nodeClass[j].getDelay()) && (nodeClass[i].getID() == nodeClass[j].getID()))  // Has to be aprt of the same getDelay 
node for the specific flight getID 
                { 
                     
                    Arcs newArc("Flight","Delay",i,j, nodeClass[i].getAirport(), nodeClass[j].getAirport(), 
nodeClass[i].getID(),nodeClass[i].getAir(), nodeClass[i].getFleet(), nodeClass[i].getCap(), nodeClass[i].getDuty(), 
nodeClass[i].getDelay()); 
                    arcClass.push_back(newArc); 
                     
                     
                     
                } 
                 
                 
                 
            } 
             
        } 
         
         
    } 
     
     
     
     
     
} 
 
 
// Create flight arcs for different types (flight, maintenance etc) --------------------------------------- 
 
void createArcs_Flight(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass, string type){ 
     
    int dep[size]; 
    int des[size]; 
    string str_dep[size]; 
    string str_des[size]; 
    string id_dep[size]; 
    string id_des[size]; 
    string air[size]; 
    string fleet[size]; 
    string captain[size]; 
    string duty[size]; 
     
     
    int j1 = 0; 
    int j2 = 0; 
     
    // Test if the node is of type "type" and departure/arrival 
     
    for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++){ 
         
        if((nodeClass[i].getType2 () == type) && (nodeClass[i].getType1() == "Departure")){ // Is it a type departure 
node? 
             
            dep[j1] = i; 
            str_dep[j1] = nodeClass[i].getAirport(); 
            id_dep[j1] = nodeClass[i].getID(); 
            air[j1] = nodeClass[i].getAir(); 
            fleet[j1] = nodeClass[i].getFleet(); 
            captain[j1] = nodeClass[i].getCap(); 
            duty[j1] = nodeClass[i].getDuty(); 
            j1++; 
             
        } else if((nodeClass[i].getType2 () == type) && (nodeClass[i].getType1() == "Arrival")){ // Is it a type 
==PAGE:161==
arrival node? 
             
            des[j2] = i; 
            id_des[j2] = nodeClass[i].getID(); 
            str_des[j2] = nodeClass[i].getAirport(); 
            captain[j2] = nodeClass[i].getCap(); 
            duty[j2] = nodeClass[i].getDuty(); 
            j2++; 
             
             
        } 
    } 
     
    if (j1 !=0){ // Only create arcs if both nodes exist 
        for (int i = 0; i < j2; i++){ 
            if((type != "Maintenance")){ 
                Arcs newArc("Flight",type,dep[i],des[i], str_dep[i], str_des[i], id_dep[i], air[i], fleet[i], 
captain[i], duty[i], 0); 
                arcClass.push_back(newArc); 
                 
            } else { 
                Arcs newArc("Maintenance","Original",dep[i],des[i], str_dep[i], str_des[i], id_dep[i], air[i], 
fleet[i],captain[i], duty[i], 0); 
                arcClass.push_back(newArc); 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
} 
 
 
 
// Create arcs between arrival to first possible departure 
 
 
void createArcs_first(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass){ 
     
    string type; 
     
     
    for(unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++){ 
        if ((firstIndex[i] != -1) && (nodeClass[i].getTime() >= rec_start-1)){  // rec_start - 1 to ensure feasibility 
with recovery window 
             
            if ((nodeClass[i].getType2() == "Original") && (nodeClass[firstIndex[i]].getType2() == "Original") && 
(nodeClass[i].getAir() == nodeClass[firstIndex[i]].getAir())){ 
                 
                type = "Original"; 
                 
            } else { 
                 
                type = "First"; 
            } 
             
            // From node i, to the first node, node i can be connect to through the firstIndex parameter 
             
            Arcs newArc("Ground", type, i, firstIndex[i], nodeClass[i].getAirport(), nodeClass[i].getAirport(), "-", "-
", "-", "- ", "-"); 
            arcClass.push_back(newArc); 
        } 
    } 
} 
 
 
// Identify all departure nodes at a given airport, and make connection between them 
 
void air_dep(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass, string airport){ 
     
    int index[nodeClass.size()]; // Size of storing index 
     
    int i = 0;  // Initialise counter 
    int v; 
     
    for (int j = 0; j < nodeClass.size(); j++) 
    { 
         
        if((nodeClass[j].getAirport() == airport) && (nodeClass[j].getType1() == "Departure") && 
(nodeClass[j].getTime() >= rec_start)) 
        { 
             
            v = j; 
            index[i] = v;  // Identify with time for all departure nodes 
            i++; 
             
             
        } 
         
         
    } 
     
     
    for (int j = 0; j < i-1; j++) 
==PAGE:162==
    { 
        for (int jj = j + 1; jj < i; jj++) 
        { 
            int temp; 
             
            if (nodeClass[index[j]].getTime() > nodeClass[index[jj]].getTime())   // Sort based on time value 
            { 
                temp = index[j]; 
                index[j] = index[jj]; 
                index[jj] = temp; 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
    for (int j = 1; j < i; j++) 
    { 
         
        Arcs newArc("Ground","Sequential",index[j-1],index[j],nodeClass[index[j-1]].getAirport(),nodeClass[index[j-
1]].getAirport(), "-", "-", "-", "-", "-"); 
        arcClass.push_back(newArc); 
    } 
     
     
} 
 
 
 
// Identify the index of first departure used in createArcs_first 
 
void first_departure(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass){ 
     
    int time;  // set to big value 
    int v; 
     
     
    for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++){                // An arrival node 
         
        firstIndex[i]= -1; 
         
        time = 20000; 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < nodeClass.size(); j++){            // A departure node ahead in time 
             
            if( (nodeClass[i].getType1() == "Arrival") && (nodeClass[j].getType1() == "Departure") && 
(nodeClass[i].getAirport() == nodeClass[j].getAirport())) { 
                 
                if ((nodeClass[i].getType2() != "Source") && (nodeClass[j].getType2() != "Sink")){ 
                     
                    if ((nodeClass[i].getTime() + turntime < nodeClass[j].getTime()) && (nodeClass[j].getTime() < 
time)) { 
                         
                        v = j; 
                        time = nodeClass[j].getTime(); 
                        firstIndex[i] = v; 
                    } 
                } else {  // Turn time should not be considered if we are dealing with a source/arrival or 
departure/sink node 
                     
                    if ((nodeClass[i].getTime() < nodeClass[j].getTime()) && (nodeClass[j].getTime() < time)) { 
                         
                        v = j; 
                        time = nodeClass[j].getTime(); 
                        firstIndex[i] = v; 
                    } 
                     
                     
                } 
                 
                 
            } 
             
             
        } 
         
    } 
     
}

        time = 20000; 
         
        for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++){ 
             
            if ((nodeClass[i].getType2() != "Delay")){

                if(nodeClass[i].getAir() == aircrafts[j]){    // If aircraft is matched 
                     
                    if(nodeClass[i].getTime() <= time){        // If time is smaller than previous time 
                         
                        rec_source[j] = i;                     // Store the node number 
                         
                        time = nodeClass[i].getTime(); 
                    } 
                } 
            } 
             
        } 
         
    } 
     
} 
 
// Identify the last activitiy for each aircraft ---------------------------------------------------------------- 
 
void rec_sink_index(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass) {

                        time = nodeClass[i].getTime(); 
                    } 
                } 
             
        } 
         
    } 
     
} 
 
// Identify the last activity for each aircraft before recovery window ------------------------------------------ 
 
void rec_source_index2(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass) { 
     
    int time; // set to big value 
     
    for (int j = 0; j < nbAircraft; j++) { 
         
        time = 0;

matched 
                 
                if(nodeClass[i].getTime() > time){        // If time is bigger than previous time 
                     
                    rec_source2[j] = i; 
                     
                    time = nodeClass[i].getTime(); 
                } 
            } 
             
        } 
         
         
    } 
     
} 
 
// Identify first activity for aircraft after recovery ends 
 
 
void rec_after_index(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass) { 
     
    int time; // set to big value 
     
    for (int j = 0; j < nbAircraft; j++) { 
         
        time = 20000; 
         
        for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++){ 
             
            if(nodeClass[i].getAir() == aircrafts[j] && (nodeClass[i].getTime() > rec_end))  // First activity for each 
aircraft after rec window

            { 
                 
                if(nodeClass[i].getTime() <= time)          // If time is less than previous time 
                { 
                     
                    rec_after[j] = i;                       // Store the node number 
                     
                    time = nodeClass[i].getTime(); 
                } 
            } 
             
        } 
         
        cout << aircrafts[j] << " : " << rec_after[j] << endl; 
         
    } 
} 
     
 
 
// Create node at the border of the recovery window if last activity was before the end of the recovery window 
identified ----------------- 
 
void sink_arc_node(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass) { 
     
    for (int j = 0; j < nbAirports; j++) { 
         
        Nodes newNode("Departure", "Collection", airports[j], rec_end, "-", "ForAll", "-", "-", "-"); 
        nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
    } 
     
     
} 
 
// Create special demand-arcs to connect departure nodes (sink_arc_node) to the common sink outside of recovery window 
(rec_sink_nodes) ----- 
 
void sink_arc(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass) { 
     
         
        for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++)  // Departure 
        { 
             
            for (unsigned int j = 0; j < nodeClass.size(); j++) // Arrival 
            { 
                 
             
            if ((nodeClass[i].getAir() == "ForAll") && (nodeClass[j].getType2() == "Sink") && (nodeClass[j].getID() == 
"Special")) 
            { 
                
                Arcs newArc("Ground","Demand",i,j,nodeClass[i].getAirport(),nodeClass[i].getAirport(), "-", "_", "-",  
"-", "-"); 
                arcClass.push_back(newArc); 
                 
            } 
             
  
             
            } 
         
        } 
     
     
} 
 
// Create source nodes 
 
void rec_source_nodes(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass){ 
     
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) { 
         
        if ((rec_source2[i] == 0) && (nodeClass[rec_source[i]].getTime() >= rec_start)) // First activity after 
recovery window begins then rec_source 
        { 
             
            if ((nodeClass[rec_source[i]].getType2() == "Maintenance"))   // Place just before 
            { 
                 
                Nodes newNode("Arrival", "Source", nodeClass[rec_source[i]].getAirport(), rec_start-0.5, "-", 
aircrafts[i], "-","-",  "-"); 
                nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
             
            } else { 
                 
                if (nodeClass[rec_source[i]].getTime() == rec_start)  // If borderline -  initiate it right before 
                { 
                     
                    Nodes newNode("Arrival", "Source", nodeClass[rec_source[i]].getAirport(), rec_start-0.5, "-", 
aircrafts[i], "-", "_", "-"); 
                    nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
==PAGE:165==
                     
                     
                } else { 
                 
                Nodes newNode("Arrival", "Source", nodeClass[rec_source[i]].getAirport(), rec_start, "-", aircrafts[i], 
"-", "-", "-"); 
                nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
                 
                } 
                 
            } 
             
             
        } else {  // First activity before recovery window begins - place source according to rec_source2 (last 
activity before rec window) 
         
         
        if (nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getType1() == "Departure") { // Departure case 
             
            Nodes newNode("Arrival", "Source", nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getAirport(), 
nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getTime()-10, "-", aircrafts[i], "-", "-",  "-"); 
            nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
             
        } 
         
        if (nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getType1() == "Arrival") {    // Arrival case 
             
            if (rec_start - nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getTime() >= turntime){ // Ensure compliance with turn times 
             
                Nodes newNode("Arrival", "Source", nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getAirport(), rec_start, "-", 
aircrafts[i], "-", "-", "-"); 
                nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
                 
            } else { 
                 
                Nodes newNode("Arrival", "Source", nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getAirport(), 
nodeClass[rec_source2[i]].getTime()+turntime, "-", aircrafts[i],"-", "-",  "-"); 
                nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
            } 
             
        } 
         
         
         
        } 
    } 
     
     
} 
 
void rec_sink_nodes(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass){ 
     
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
    { 
         
        // Special case where there is plenty of time, however the aircraft need to be at the respective airport 
         
        if ((nodeClass[rec_after[i]].getType1() == "Departure") && (nodeClass[rec_after[i]].getTime() >= rec_end + 
turntime)) 
        { 
 
            Nodes newNode("Departure", "Sink", nodeClass[rec_after[i]].getAirport(), rec_end+turntime/2-i*0.02, "-", 
aircrafts[i], "-", "-", "-"); 
            nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
 
        } 
     
        else // All other cases 
         
        { 
            if  ((nodeClass[rec_sink[i]].getType1() == "Arrival") && (nodeClass[rec_sink[i]].getTime() <= rec_end)) 
            { 
                // special to create demand connect 
                 
                Nodes newNode("Departure", "Sink", nodeClass[rec_sink[i]].getAirport(), rec_end+10, "Special", 
aircrafts[i], "-", "_",  "-"); 
                nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
                 
            } 
             
            if  ((nodeClass[rec_sink[i]].getType1() == "Arrival") && (nodeClass[rec_sink[i]].getTime() > rec_end)) 
            { 
                // to create nodes in the end/end 
                 
                Nodes newNode("Departure", "Sink", nodeClass[rec_sink[i]].getAirport(), 
nodeClass[rec_sink[i]].getTime() + 10, "-", aircrafts[i], "-", "-", "-"); 
                nodeClass.push_back(newNode); 
            } 
 
         
        } 
==PAGE:166==
         
    } 
     
} 
 
 
// Create disruption scenario 
 
void disruption(int i, int a, IloNumVarArray2 var_x, IloModel model) 
{ 
    model.add(var_x[i][a] == 0); 
 
}

#ifndef createMatrices_h 
#define createMatrices_h 
 
#include <iostream> 
#include <fstream> 
#include <string> 
#include <sstream> 
#include <vector> 
#include <iomanip> 
 
 
#include "parameters.h" 
#include "nodes.hpp" 
#include "arcs.hpp" 
 
 
// Create directed adjacency relation between nodes (which are connected to one another) -------------------------- 
 
void adj_alloc(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass){ 
     
    for (unsigned int j= 0; j < nodeClass.size(); j++){ 
         
        for(unsigned int i = 0; i < arcClass.size();i++){ 
             
            if (arcClass[i].getDepNode() == j){ 
                 
                aux_Adj.push_back(arcClass[i].getArrNode()); // All arrival nodes from node j 
            } 
        } 
        Adj.push_back(aux_Adj); 
        aux_Adj.clear();            // Delete all elements of aux_Adj in order to reuse it 
    } 
     
} 
 
 
// Identify original flights to aircraft --------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
 
void org_alloc(vector<Arcs>& arcClass){ 
     
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft;i++){ 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < arcClass.size(); j++){ 
             
            if ((aircrafts[i] == arcClass[j].getAir()) && (arcClass[j].getType2() == "Original")) 
            { 
                 
                Org[i].push_back(j); 
                 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
} 
 
// Identify original captain to arcs --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
 
 
void org_alloc_cap(vector<Arcs>& arcClass){ 
     
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbCaptains;i++){ 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < arcClass.size(); j++){ 
             
            if ((captains[i] == arcClass[j].getCap()) && (arcClass[j].getType2() == "Original")) 
            { 
                 
                Orgcap[i].push_back(j); 
                 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
} 
 
 
 
// Assign costs to each arc for every aircraft in relation to fleet type etc. -------------------------------------- 
 
void cost_alloc(vector<Arcs>& arcClass){ 
     
==PAGE:168==
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < arcClass.size(); j++){ 
             
            if (arcClass[j].getType1() == "Flight")     // Only assign cost to flights (not ground) 
            { 
                if ((arcClass[j].getAir() == aircrafts[i]) && (arcClass[j].getType2() == "Original")) 
                { 
                    cost_arc[i].push_back(j); 
                    cost_factor[i].push_back(1);  // Symbolic value to verify formulation 
                } 
                 
                if ((arcClass[j].getAir() != aircrafts[i]) && (arcClass[j].getFleet() == fleetReq[i])) 
                { 
                    cost_arc[i].push_back(j); 
                    cost_factor[i].push_back(cSwap+arcClass[j].getDelay()*cDelay); 
                } 
                 
                if ((arcClass[j].getAir() != aircrafts[i]) && (arcClass[j].getFleet() != fleetReq[i])) 
                { 
                    cost_arc[i].push_back(j); 
                    cost_factor[i].push_back(cFleetSwap+arcClass[j].getDelay()*cDelay); 
                } 
                 
                 
                if ((arcClass[j].getAir() == aircrafts[i]) && (arcClass[j].getType2() == "Delay")) 
                { 
                    cost_arc[i].push_back(j); 
                    cost_factor[i].push_back(cDelay*arcClass[j].getDelay()); 
                } 
                 
                 
            } 
             
        } 
     
     
     
} 
 
// Identify flight ID to arcs --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
 
void flight_alloc(vector<Arcs>& arcClass){ 
     
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbFlights; i++) 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < arcClass.size(); j++){ 
             
            if (arcClass[j].getType1() == "Flight")     // Only assign cost to flights (not ground) 
            { 
                if ((arcClass[j].getID() == flightRoute[i])) 
                { 
                    fl_arc[i].push_back(j); 
                } 
                 
            } 
             
        } 
     
     
     
} 
 
// Identify source and sink nodes for all aircraft ----------------------------------------------------------------- 
 
void demand_alloc(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass){ 
     
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < nodeClass.size(); j++){ 
             
            if ((nodeClass[j].getAir() == aircrafts[i]) && (nodeClass[j].getType2() == "Source"))     // Assign for 
source nodes 
            { 
                dem_arc[i].push_back(j); 
                dem_factor[i].push_back(1); // Source is a 1 
                 
            } 
            if ((nodeClass[j].getAir() == aircrafts[i]) && (nodeClass[j].getType2() == "Sink"))     // Assign for sink 
nodes 
            { 
                dem_arc[i].push_back(j); 
                dem_factor[i].push_back(-1); // Sink is a -1 
                 
            } 
             
        } 
     
}

// Identify all in-going arcs for every node 
 
 
void in_go(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass) 
{ 
     
    for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++) 
    { 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < arcClass.size(); j++) 
        { 
            if (arcClass[j].getArrNode() == i) { 
                 
                v_in_aux.push_back(j); 
                 
            } 
             
        } 
        v_in.push_back(v_in_aux); 
        v_in_aux.clear(); 
         
    } 
     
     
} 
 
 
 
// Identfy all out-going arcs for every node 
 
void out_go(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass) 
{ 
     
    for (unsigned int i = 0; i < nodeClass.size(); i++) 
    { 
         
        for (unsigned int j = 0; j < arcClass.size(); j++) 
        { 
            if (arcClass[j].getDepNode() == i) { 
                 
                v_out_aux.push_back(j); 
                 
            } 
             
        } 
        v_out.push_back(v_out_aux); 
        v_out_aux.clear(); 
         
    } 
     
     
} 
 
// Identify all arcs that should be fixed to aircraft 
 
void fix_air(vector<Nodes>& nodeClass, vector<Arcs>& arcClass) 
{ 
     
     
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbAircraft; i++) 
     
    { 
         
        for (unsigned int a = 0; a < arcClass.size(); a++) 
         
        { 
                if (arcClass[a].getAir() == aircrafts[i])           // Arc and Aircraft should match 
                { 
                     
                    if (arcClass[a].getType1() == "Maintenance")    // Case 1: Fix maintenance arcs 
                    { 
                         
                        fix[i].push_back(a);                        // Store a 
                         
                         
                    } 
                     
                    if ((arcClass[a].getType1() == "Flight") && (arcClass[a].getType2() == "Original") // Case 2: Fix 
non-recovery window arcs to original schedule 
                        && ((nodeClass[arcClass[a].getDepNode()].getTime() >= rec_end) 
                            || (nodeClass[arcClass[a].getDepNode()].getTime() < rec_start) || 
((nodeClass[arcClass[a].getArrNode()].getTime() >= rec_end) && (nodeClass[arcClass[a].getDepNode()].getTime() >= 
rec_start)))) 
                    { 
                         
                        fix[i].push_back(a);                        // Store a 
                         
                         
                    }

                } 
         
        } 
         
         
    } 
     
     
}

#ifndef crew_h 
#define crew_h 
 
#include "parameters.h" 
#include "arcs.hpp" 
#include "nodes.hpp" 
#include "corr.hpp" 
 
 
// Function that initialises everything regarding crew 
 
void crew_start(void) 
{ 
     
 
    // Because double up appears - wenneed to delete duplicate values 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbCaptains; i++) 
    { 
        cap_duty[i].erase(unique(cap_duty[i].begin(), cap_duty[i].end()),cap_duty[i].end()); // Erase non-unique values 
    } 
     
    
     
    int end_duty[nbDuties]; 
     
    // Identify start time of duty / if original 
     
    cout << "DUTIES" << endl; 
    for (int i = 0; i < nbDuties; i++) 
    { 
         
        start_duty[i] = 10000; 
         
        for (unsigned int n = 0; n < allNodes.size(); n++) 
        { 
             
            for (int j = 0; j < id_duty[i].size(); j++) 
            { 
                if ((allNodes[n].getType2() == "Original") && (allNodes[n].getID() == id_duty[i][j]) && 
(allNodes[n].getType1() == "Departure")) // The first one must be the earliest 
                { 
                    if (allNodes[n].getTime() < start_duty[i]) 
                    { 
                        start_duty[i] = allNodes[n].getTime(); 
                        cout << duties[i] << " " << start_duty[i] << endl; 
                    } 
                } 
            } 
             
        } 
         
    } 
     
 
 
 
     
    // Assign duty numbers to captains (vector <int>) 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbCaptains; i++)               // For each captain 
    { 
        for (int j = 0; j < cap_duty[i].size();j++)    // Look up the assigned duties 
        { 
            for (int d = 0; d < nbDuties; d++)         // Calculate the difference between their start and end times 
            { 
                if (duties[d] == cap_duty[i][j]) 
                { 
                    cap_duty_nb[i].push_back(d); 
                     
//                    cout << captains[i]<< " " << d << endl; 
                } 
            } 
        } 
    } 
     
cout << endl; 
    } 
     
 
}

void crew_end(vector<Corr>& allCorr) 
{ 
    // Crew considerations 
    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) 
    { 
        cout << "-----"; 
    } 
    cout << endl; 
    cout << "CREW CONSIDERATIONS " << endl; 
    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) 
    { 
        cout << "-----"; 
    } 
    cout << endl; 
    cout << setw(25) << left << "Minimum connection time: " << setw(6) << right << connect_Time << " minutes" << endl; 
    cout << setw(25) << left << "Maximum duty time: " << setw(6) << right << duty_Time << " minutes (" << duty_Time/60 
<< " hours) " << endl; 
    cout << setw(25) << left << "Minimum rest time: " << setw(6) << right << rest_Time << " minutes (" << rest_Time/60 
<< " hours) " << endl; 
    cout << endl; 
    cout << "Original schedule " << endl; 
    cout << "-----------------------------" << endl << endl; 
     
    for (int i = 0; i < nbCaptains; i++) 
    { 
        cout << captains[i] << " (" << cap_duty[i].size() << " duties) (" << rest[i].size() << " rest period(s))" << 
endl; 
         
        for (int j = 0; j < cap_duty[i].size();j++)  // CAPTAIN TO DUTY 
        { 
            cout << setw(5) << right << j+1 << "." << cap_duty[i][j] << endl; 
             
            for (int d = 0; d < nbDuties; d++) 
            { 
                if (cap_duty[i][j] == duties[d]) 
                { 
                    for (int c = 0; c < id_duty[d].size(); c++)   // DUTY TO ID 
                    { 
                         
                        cout << setw(7) << right << "-" << id_duty[d][c] << endl; 
                         
                        for (int f = 0; f < nbFlights; f++) 
                        { 
                            for (int a = 0; a < fl_arc[f].size(); a++) 
                            { 
                                if (id_duty[d][c] == flightRoute[f]) 
                                { 
                                    cout << setw(10) << right << ". " << fl_arc[f][a] << endl; 
                                     
                                    Corr newCorr(captains[i], cap_duty[i][j], id_duty[d][c], fl_arc[f][a]); 
                                    allCorr.push_back(newCorr); 
                                     
                                     
                                } 
                            } 
                             
                             
                        } 
                    } 
                } 
            } 
        } 
        cout << endl; 
         
    } 
    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) 
    { 
        cout << "-----"; 
    } 
    cout << endl; 
} 
 
void crew_matrix(vector<Corr>& corr, vector<Nodes>& nodes, vector<Arcs>& arcs) 
{ 
     
     
     
 
    int k; 
     
 
    // Determine which arcs are not legal for a Captains duty 
     
    cout << "Duty" << endl; 
     
    for (int d = 0; d < nbDuties; d++) 
    { 
         
         
        for (unsigned int c = 0; c < corr.size(); c++) 
        { 
             
==PAGE:180==
            if (corr[c].getDuty() == duties[d]) 
            { 
                k = nodes[arcs[corr[c].getArc()].getArrNode()].getTime() - start_duty[d]; 
                 
                if (k > duty_Time) 
                { 
                    arc1_duty.push_back(corr[c].getArc()); 
                     
                    cout << "For " << duties[d] << " "  << start_duty[d] << " ID: "<< corr[c].getID() << " ARC:" << 
corr[c].getArc() << endl; 
                } 
            } 
             
             
        } 
    } 
 
     
    // Need to create constraints between duties for the rest periods 
     
    cout << "Rest time" << endl; 
    for (unsigned int d = 0; d < corr.size(); d++) // The first one 
    { 
        for (unsigned int c = 0; c < corr.size(); c++) // The second one 
        { 
             
            // Same captain, different duties, d comes before c (d = arrival and c = depature) 
             
            if( (corr[d].getCap() == corr[c].getCap()) && (corr[d].getDuty() != corr[c].getDuty()) 
               && (nodes[arcs[corr[d].getArc()].getArrNode()].getTime() < 
nodes[arcs[corr[c].getArc()].getDepNode()].getTime())) 
               { 
                   k = nodes[arcs[corr[c].getArc()].getDepNode()].getTime() - 
nodes[arcs[corr[d].getArc()].getArrNode()].getTime(); 
                   if (k < rest_Time) // Rest time 
                   { 
                       cout <<  "From : " << corr[d].getID() << " (" << corr[d].getArc() << ") to " << corr[c].getID() 
<< " (" << corr[c].getArc() << ")" << endl; 
                       cout <<  k << endl; 
                       arc1_rest.push_back(corr[d].getArc()); 
                       arc2_rest.push_back(corr[c].getArc()); 
                   } 
                    
               } 
        } 
    } 
     
    // Need to create constraints between ids for connection times 
     
    cout << "Connection time" << endl; 
    for (unsigned int d = 0; d < corr.size(); d++) // The first one 
    { 
        for (unsigned int c = 0; c < corr.size(); c++) // The second one 
        { 
          
            // Same captain, different IDs, same duty , d comes before c (d = arrival, c = departure) 
             
            if ( (corr[d].getCap() == corr[c].getCap()) && (corr[d].getID() != corr[c].getID()) && 
                (corr[d].getDuty() == corr[c].getDuty()) && 
                (nodes[arcs[corr[d].getArc()].getDepNode()].getTime() < 
nodes[arcs[corr[c].getArc()].getDepNode()].getTime())) 
            { 
                k = nodes[arcs[corr[c].getArc()].getDepNode()].getTime() - 
nodes[arcs[corr[d].getArc()].getArrNode()].getTime(); 
                if (k < connect_Time) // Connection time 
                { 
                    cout <<  "From : " << corr[d].getID() << " (" << corr[d].getArc() << ") to " << corr[c].getID() << 
" (" << corr[c].getArc() << ")" << endl; 
                    cout <<  k << endl; 
                    arc1_connect.push_back(corr[d].getArc()); 
                    arc2_connect.push_back(corr[c].getArc()); 
                } 
 
                 
            } 
             
             
        } 
    } 
     
     
}

#include "corr.hpp" 
 
 
// Constructors 
 
Corr::Corr(){ 
    newCap = " "; 
} 
 
Corr::Corr(string captain, string duty, string id, int arc){ 
    newCap = captain; 
    newDuty = duty; 
    newID = id; 
    newArc = arc; 
} 
 
 
// Getters --------------------------------- 
 
string Corr::getCap() const{ 
    return newCap; 
} 
 
string Corr::getDuty() const{ 
    return newDuty; 
} 
 
string Corr::getID() const{ 
    return newID; 
} 
 
int Corr::getArc() const{ 
    return newArc; 
} 
 
 
 
 
// Setters --------------------------------- 
 
void Corr::setCap(string captain){ 
    newCap = captain; 
} 
 
void Corr::setDuty(string duty){ 
    newDuty = duty; 
} 
 
void Corr::setID(string id){ 
    newID = id; 
} 
 
void Corr::setArc(int arc){ 
    newArc = arc; 
}
